class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">L</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0315em;">k</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0077em;">R</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0315em;">k</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>. The
zero-order-hold discrete model over <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Δ</mi><mi>t</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>20</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\Delta t = 20</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">Δ</span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">20</span></span></span></span>&nbsp;ms is computed from a truncated matrix
exponential:
</p>

<div class="eq"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>A</mi><mrow><mi>d</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msub><mtext>  </mtext><mo>=</mo><mtext>  </mtext><mn mathvariant="bold">1</mn><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Δ</mi><mi>t</mi><mtext> </mtext><msub><mi>A</mi><mrow><mi>c</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msub><mo>+</mo><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mn>2</mn></mfrac></mstyle><mi mathvariant="normal">Δ</mi><msup><mi>t</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><msubsup><mi>A</mi><mrow><mi>c</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow><mn>2</mn></msubsup><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="2em"/><msub><mi>B</mi><mrow><mi>d</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msub><mtext>  </mtext><mo>=</mo><mtext>  </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">Δ</mi><mi>t</mi><mtext> </mtext><msub><mi>B</mi><mrow><mi>c</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msub><mo>+</mo><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mn>2</mn></mfrac></mstyle><mi mathvariant="normal">Δ</mi><msup><mi>t</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><msub><mi>A</mi><mrow><mi>c</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msub><msub><mi>B</mi><mrow><mi>c</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msub><mo>+</mo><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mn>6</mn></mfrac></mstyle><mi mathvariant="normal">Δ</mi><msup><mi>t</mi><mn>3</mn></msup><msubsup><mi>A</mi><mrow><mi>c</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow><mn>2</mn></msubsup><msub><mi>B</mi><mrow><mi>c</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A_{d,k} \;=\; \mathbf{1} + \Delta t\, A_{c,k} + \tfrac{1}{2}\Delta t^2 A_{c,k}^2,
\qquad
B_{d,k} \;=\; \Delta t\, B_{c,k} + \tfrac{1}{2}\Delta t^2 A_{c,k} B_{c,k}
 + \tfrac{1}{6}\Delta t^3 A_{c,k}^2 B_{c,k}.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9694em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span <p>
<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>A</mi><mi>c</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A_c</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> here is nilpotent-like in structure (orientation ← angular velocity ← nothing;
position ← velocity ← gravity), so the truncation error at these magnitudes is negligible while
avoiding a general <code>expm</code> — a small example of a recurring theme: the SRB structure is
simple enough that exploiting it by hand beats calling the general-purpose routine.
</p>

<h3 id="condensed-qp">4.2&ensp;Condensing the horizon</h3>

<p>
Rather than keeping states as decision variables with dynamics as equality constraints, the
horizon is condensed: the stacked state prediction

</p>

<div class="eq"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi <p>with the lifted matrices built from per-step transition products — the LTV generalization of
the constant-matrix condensing in [1]:</p>

<div class="eq"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>A</mi><mrow><mi scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">Φ</mi><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A_{\mathrm{qp}} =
\begin{bmatrix}
\Phi_{1,0} \\ \Phi_{2,0} \\ \vdots \\ \Phi_{H,0}
\end{bmatrix},
\qquad
[B_{\mathrm{qp}}]_{kj} =
\begin{cases}
\Phi_{k, j+1}\, B_{d,j}, &amp; j &lt; k\\[2pt]
\mathbf{0}, &amp; j \ge k
\end{cases}
\qquad
\Phi_{k,j} \;=\; A_{d,k-1} A_{d,k-2} \cdots A_{d,j}.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9694em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">qp</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:5.46em;vertical-align:-2.48em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen"><span class="delimsizing mult"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:2.95em;"><span style="top:-4.95em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:7.4em;"></span><span style="width:0.667em;height:5.4em;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.667em" height="5.4em" viewBox="0 0 667 5400"><path d="M403 1759 V84 H666 V0 H319 V1759 v1800 v1759 v84 h347 v-84

<p>
The payoff is size: the decision vector shrinks to the wrenches alone (<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>12</mn><mi>H</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>300</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">12H = 300</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">12</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0813em;">H</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">300</span></span></span></span> variables for
<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">=</mo><mn>25</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">H{=}25</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0813em;">H</span><span class="mord"><span class="mrel">=</span></span><span class="mord">25</span></span></span></span>), swing-foot wrenches are eliminated by cheap equality rows rather than extra states,
and the Hessian dimension is independent of the state dimension. The cost is that <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>B</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">q</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B_{\mathrm{qp}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9694em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0502em;">B</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0502em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">qp</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>
is dense — which is embraced rather than fought; <a href="#solver">§10</a> shows where the
sparsity that <em>does</em> exist is spent.
</p>

<p>The tracking objective is the weighted least-squares deviation plus a wrench-magnitude penalty,</p>

<div class="eq"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>J</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">U</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo fence="false" stretchy="true" minsize="1.2em" maxsize="1.2em">∥</mo><msub><mi>A</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">q</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi></mrow></msub><msub><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>B</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">q</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi></mrow></msub><mi mathvariant="bold">U</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">r</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">e</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">f</mi></mrow></msub><msubsup><mo fence="false" stretchy="true" minsize="1.2em" maxsize="1.2em">∥</mo><mi>L</mi><mn>2</mn></msubsup><mo>+</mo><mo stretchy="false">∥</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">U</mi><msubsup><mo stretchy="false">∥</mo><mi>K</mi><mn>2</mn></msubsup><mo separator="true">,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">J(\mathbf{U})
= \big\lVert A_{\mathrm{qp}}\mathbf{x}_0 + B_{\mathrm{qp}}\mathbf{U} - \mathbf{X}_{\mathrm{ref}} \big\rVert_{L}^{2}
+ \lVert \mathbf{U} \rVert_{K}^{2},</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0962em;">J</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathbf">U</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.2em;vertical-align:-0.35em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="delimsizing mult"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.85em;"><span style="top:-2.85em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3.2em;"></span><span style="width:0.556em;height:1.2em;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.556em" height="1.2em" viewBox="0 0 556 1200"><path d="M145 15 v585 v0 v585 c2.667,10,9.667,15,21,15

<p>
with <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>L</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">i</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">g</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>Q</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>Q</mi><mi>H</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">L = \mathrm{diag}(Q_1, \dots, Q_H)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right:0.0139em;">diag</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">Q</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3011em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">Q</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm" Expanding and dropping constants gives the standard QP data
</p>

style="height:1.2822em;vertical-align:-0.3831em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord"><span class="delimsizing size1">(</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3011em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="delimsizing size1">)</span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span></span></span></span></span></div>

<p>subject to the contact-wrench inequalities and swing-zero equalities of
<a href="#constraints">§5</a>. Only the first input <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi mathvariant="bold">u</mi><mn>0</mn><mo>∗</mo></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbf{u}_0^\ast</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9368em;vertical-align:-0.2481em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">u</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.6887em;"><span style="top:-2.4519em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span><span style="top:-3.063em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2481em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> is applied; the rest of
the horizon exists to make <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi mathvariant="bold">u</mi><mn>0</mn><mo>∗</mo></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbf{u}_0^\ast</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9368em;vertical-align:-0.2481em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">u</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.6887em;"><span style="top:-2.4519em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span><span style="top:-3.063em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2481em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> farsighted.</p>

<h3 id="cost-transform">4.3&ensp;The body-yaw cost transform</h3>

<p>
Here is a failure mode that does not exist on a robot that mostly walks straight. Suppose the
position weights are anisotropic — say lateral tracking is punished ten times harder than
longitudinal, which is typical for a narrow-footed biped. With a world-axis diagonal <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>Q</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Q</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8778em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">Q</span></span></span></span>, the
cost
</p>

<div class="eq"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>J</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">r</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">e</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">f</mi></mrow></msub><msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mrow><mtext> ⁣</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">⊤</mi></mrow></msup><msub><mi>Q</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">w</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">o</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">r</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">l</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi></mrow></msub><mtext> </mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">r</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">e</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">f</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">J = (\mathbf{x} - \mathbf{x}_{\mathrm{ref}})^{\!\top} Q_{\mathrm{world}}\, (\mathbf{x} - \mathbf{x}_{\mathrm{ref}})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0962em;">J</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathbf">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.1491em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight" style="margin-right:0.0778em;">ref</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.8991em;"><span style="top:-3.113em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mspace mtight" style="margin-right:-0.1952em;"></span><span class="mord mtight">⊤</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">Q</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">world</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathbf">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight" style="margin-right:0.0778em;">ref</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></div>

<p>
means “punish world-<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.625em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0359em;">y</span></span></span></span> error hard.” The moment the robot yaws 90°, that axis is now the robot's
<em>forward</em> direction: the controller is suddenly stiff where it should be permissive and
loose where it needs authority. Foot placement rotates with the heading, the tracking objective
does not, and the two drift apart — the classic symptom is a robot that walks straight
beautifully and feels underdamped the moment it turns.
</p>

<p>
The fix used here transforms the tracking <em>error</em> into the body-yaw frame at every horizon
step, using the <em>reference</em> yaw <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>ψ</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">r</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">e</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">f</mi></mrow><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\psi_{\mathrm{ref},k}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9805em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0359em;">ψ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0359em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight" style="margin-right:0.0778em;">ref</span></span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0315em;">k</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> — a known constant at QP-build
time:
</p>

<div class="eq"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="bold">e</mi><mi>k</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><munder><mo>∑</mo><mi>k</mi></munder><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mi>k</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><msub><mi stretchy="false">)</mo><mrow><mtext> ⁣</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">⊤</mi></mrow></msup><mtext> </mtext><munder><munder><mrow><msubsup><mi>T</mi><mi>k</mi><mrow><mtext> ⁣</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">⊤</mi></mrow></msubsup><mi>Q</mi><mtext> </mtext><msub><mi>T</mi><mi>k</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="true">⏟</mo></munder><msub><mi>Q</mi><mi>k</mi></msub></munder><mtext> </mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mi>k</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">r</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">e</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">f</mi></mrow><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbf{e}_k = T_k\,(\mathbf{x}_k - \mathbf{x}_{\mathrm{ref},k}),

<p>where <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>T</mi><mi>k</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">T_k</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">T</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0315em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> rotates exactly three blocks and leaves the rest alone:</p>

style="margin-right:0.0778em;">ref</span></span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0315em;">k</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.8991em;"><span style="top:-3.113em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">⊤</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="delimsizing size1">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></div>

<p>
acting on (orientation, position, angular velocity, linear velocity, gravity). Because <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>T</mi><mi>k</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">T_k</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">T</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0315em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>
depends only on the reference — never on the decision variables — each <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>Q</mi><mi>k</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Q_k</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8778em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">Q</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0315em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> is a constant
positive-semidefinite matrix and <strong>the problem remains a convex QP</strong>. The Euler
block stays untransformed deliberately: roll and pitch are already body-relative tilt angles,
and “rotating” raw Euler errors with a planar rotation would mix conventions. In the
implementation this is a per-step reweighting inside the QP assembly
(<code>bodyYawStateCost()</code>), costing a handful of 3×3 multiplies per step.
</p>

<h3 id="yaw-policy">4.4&ensp;Wrapped vs. unwrapped yaw</h3>

<p>
A subtler prerequisite for turning: the yaw entry of the MPC state must be <em>continuous in
time</em>, not confined to <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mo>−</mo><mi>π</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>π</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(-\pi, \pi]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0359em;">π</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0359em;">π</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span>. Define the wrap operator and the unwrapped heading
</p>

<div class="eq"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">w</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">r</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>α</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">atan2</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>sin</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mi>α</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>cos</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mi>α</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="2em"/><msub><mi>ψ</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">u</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">n</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">w</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">r</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">e</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>t</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>ψ</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>0</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><msubsup><mo>∫</mo><mn>0</mn><mi>t</mi></msubsup><mover accent="true"><mi>ψ</mi><mo>˙</mo></mover><mtext> </mtext><mi>d</mi><mi>τ</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{wrap}(\alpha) = \operatorname{atan2}(\sin\alpha, \cos\alpha),
\qquad
\psi_{\mathrm{unwrapped}}(t) = \psi(0) + \int_0^t \dot\psi\,d\tau ,</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">wrap</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.0361em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">atan2</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mop">sin</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mop">cos</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:2em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0359em;">ψ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0359em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">unwrapped</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0359em;">ψ</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:2.4554em;vertical-align:-0.9119em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mop op-symbol large-op" style="margin-right:0.4445em;position:relative;top:-0.0011em;">∫</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.5435em;"><span style="top:-1.7881em;margin-left:-0.4445em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span><span style="top:-3.8129em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.9119em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.9313em;"><span style="top:-3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0359em;">ψ</span></span><span style="top:-3.2634em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" style="left:-0.0278em;"><span class="mord">˙</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1944em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1132em;">τ</span><span class="mpunct">,</span></span></span></span></span></div>

<p>
and the policy is a two-line rule with long consequences:
<strong>subtract yaws across time only in unwrapped form; take shortest-path errors only in
wrapped form.</strong> The MPC initial state and the reference recurrence both use unwrapped yaw
— if the state estimator hands the QP <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>ψ</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mo>+</mo><mn>179</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">°</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\psi_0 = +179°</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0359em;">ψ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3011em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0359em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7778em;vertical-align:-0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">+</span><span class="mord">179°</span></span></span></span> and the reference integrates to <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>+</mo><mn>181</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">°</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">+181°</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7778em;vertical-align:-0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">+</span><span class="mord">181°</span></span></span></span>,
the error must be <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">°</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2°</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord">2°</span></span></span></span>, not <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>358</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">°</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">-358°</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7778em;vertical-align:-0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord">358°</span></span></span></span>. Feed a wrapped state into an unwrapped reference at the
<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>±</mo><mn>180</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">°</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\pm180°</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7778em;vertical-align:-0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">±</span><span class="mord">180°</span></span></span></span> seam and the QP sees a phantom full-turn error, requests a violent corrective moment,
and the robot falls over — a bug family this project eliminated by construction, storing both
representations in the state estimate and drawing every consumer from the correct one
(wrapped for UI, logs, and feedback errors; unwrapped for the MPC state, reference, and
touchdown-yaw prediction).
</p>


<h2 id="constraints"><span class="secno">5</span>Contact-Wrench Constraints for a Finite Foot</h2>

<p>
This section is the heart of the biped extension. A point foot needs one physical law — Coulomb
friction. A finite foot needs three: the force must stay inside the friction cone, the
<em>center of pressure</em> must stay inside the foot, and the free yaw moment must stay inside
the torsional friction budget. All three are naturally expressed in the foot frame <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>F</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">F</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">F</span></span></span></span>, while the
QP's decision variables live in the world frame — and the resulting frame transformation is
where a naive implementation quietly goes wrong.
</p>

<p>Per horizon step, the stacked wrench variable is ordered forces-first:</p>

<div class="eq"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="bold">u</mi><mi>k</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mtext> </mtext><munder><munder><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>L</mi><mi>x</mi></mrow></msub><mtext>  </mtext><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>L</mi><mi>y</mi></mrow></msub><mtext>  </mtext><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>L</mi><mi>z</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="true">⏟</mo></munder><mn>0..2</mn></munder><mtext>  </mtext><munder><munder><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>R</mi><mi>x</mi></mrow></msub><mtext>  </mtext><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>R</mi><mi>y</mi></mrow></msub><mtext>  </mtext><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>R</mi><mi>z</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="true">⏟</mo></munder><mn>3..5</mn></munder><mtext>  </mtext><munder><munder><mrow><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>L</mi><mi>x</mi></mrow></msub><mtext>  </mtext><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>L</mi><mi>y</mi></mrow></msub><mtext>  </mtext><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>L</mi><mi>z</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="true">⏟</mo></munder><mn>6..8</mn></munder><mtext>  </mtext><munder><munder><mrow><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>R</mi><mi>x</mi></mrow></msub><mtext>  </mtext><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>R</mi><mi>y</mi></mrow></msub><mtext>  </mtext><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>R</mi><mi>z</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="true">⏟</mo></munder><mn>9..11</mn></munder><mtext> </mtext><msubsup><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mi>W</mi><mrow><mtext> ⁣</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">⊤</mi></mrow></msubsup><mo separator="true">,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbf{u}_k =
[\,\underbrace{F_{Lx}\; F_{Ly}\; F_{Lz}}_{0..2}\;
\underbrace{F_{Rx}\; F_{Ry}\; F_{Rz}}_{3..5}\;
\underbrace{M_{Lx}\; M_{Ly}\; M_{Lz}}_{6..8}\;
\underbrace{M_{Rx}\; M_{Ry}\; M_{Rz}}_{9..11}\,]^{\!\top}_{W},</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.5944em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">u</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0315em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:2.4843em;vertical-align:-1.5852em;"></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="minner munder"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.6833em;"><span style="top:-1.4148em;"><span class="mpunct">,</span></span></span></span></span></div>

<p>
so each foot's 6D wrench occupies the column sets <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>1</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>2</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>6</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>7</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>8</mn><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{0,1,2,6,7,8\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">6</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">7</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">8</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span> (left) and
<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mn>3</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>4</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>5</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>9</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>10</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>11</mn><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{3,4,5,9,10,11\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">3</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">4</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">5</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">9</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">10</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">11</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span> (right) — bookkeeping that matters once the constraint matrix goes sparse
(<a href="#solver">§10</a>).
</p>

<h3 id="friction-pyramid">5.1&ensp;Friction pyramid and normal-force bounds</h3>

<p>In the foot frame, Coulomb friction bounds the tangential force inside a circular cone,</p>

<div class="eq"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msqrt><mrow><msubsup><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow><mn>2</mn></msubsup><mo>+</mo><msubsup><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>y</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mrow></msqrt><mtext>  </mtext><mo>≤</mo><mtext>  </mtext><mi>μ</mi><mtext> </mtext><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="2em"/><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo>≥</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\sqrt{F_{x,F}^2 + F_{y,F}^2} \;\le\; \mu\, F_{z,F},
\qquad F_{z,F} \ge 0,</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" <p>which is second-order and therefore linearized to the inscribed pyramid — four rows:</p>

<div class="eq"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mo>±</mo><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo>−</mo><mi>μ</mi><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="2em"/><mo>±</mo><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>y</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo>−</mo><mi>μ</mi><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo>≤</mo><mn>0.</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\pm F_{x,F} - \mu F_{z,F} \le 0,

<p>Two more rows box the normal force,</p>

<div class="eq"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" \le F_{\max},</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span style="height:0.9694em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">F</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" <p>
with <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mi>min</mi><mo>⁡</mo></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>5</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">F_{\min} = 5</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">F</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3175em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mop mtight"><span class="mtight">m</span><span class="mtight">i</span><span class="mtight">n</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">5</span></span></span></span>&nbsp;N and <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mi>max</mi><mo>⁡</mo></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>1500</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">F_{\max} = 1500</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">F</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mop mtight"><span class="mtight">m</span><span class="mtight">a</span><span class="mtight">x</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1500</span></span></span></span>&nbsp;N in the MIT tuning. The lower bound is not
cosmetic: forcing a strictly positive normal force on every scheduled stance foot keeps the foot
<em>loaded</em>, which stabilizes the contact and keeps the CoP constraint below well-posed —
<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mi>z</mi></msub><mo>&gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">F_z &gt; 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">F</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.044em;">z</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&gt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span> is exactly what licenses the multiplication in <a href="#cop">§5.2</a>. During contact
transitions this bound is softened by the contact ramp (<a href="#gait">§7.5</a>).
</p>

<h3 id="cop">5.2&ensp;The center-of-pressure constraint</h3>

<figure class="diagram" role="img" aria-label="Foot support polygon diagram">
<svg viewBox="0 0 640 300" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
  <defs>
    <marker id="arr2" viewBox="0 0 10 10" refX="9" refY="5" markerWidth="7" markerHeight="7" orient="auto-start-reverse">
      <path d="M0,0 L10,5 L0,10 z" class="dg-arrow"/>
    </marker>
  </defs>
  <!-- foot rectangle (top view): x_F up (length), y_F left (width) -->

  <!-- axes from center -->
  <line x1="310" y1="150" x2="310" y2="18" class="dg-edge" marker-end="url(#arr2)"/>
  <text x="318" y="30" class="dg-math">x_F</text>

  <text x="163" y="144" class="dg-math">y_F</text>
  <circle cx="310" cy="150" r="3.2" class="dg-arrow"/>
  <text x="318" y="167" class="dg-sub">contact origin O</text>
  <!-- CoP point -->
  <circle cx="288" cy="108" r="4.5" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" class="dg-edge" stroke-width="1.8"/>
  <circle cx="288" cy="108" r="1.6" class="dg-arrow"/>
  <text x="238" y="98" class="dg-sub">CoP</text>
  <!-- half length / width markers -->
  <line x1="392" y1="150" x2="392" y2="40" class="dg-edge" stroke-dasharray="3 3"/>
  <text x="400" y="100" class="dg-math">a</text>
  <line x1="250" y1="282" x2="310" y2="282" class="dg-edge" stroke-dasharray="3 3"/>
  <text x="275" y="276" class="dg-math">b</text>
  <!-- wrench arrows -->
  <line x1="440" y1="220" x2="440" y2="120" class="dg-edge" stroke-width="1.8" marker-end="url(#arr2)"/>
  <text x="448" y="130" class="dg-math">F_z</text>
  <path d="M 470 190 a 22 22 0 1 1 10 -38" class="dg-edge" marker-end="url(#arr2)"/>
  <text x="500" y="160" class="dg-math">M_x, M_y</text>
  <text x="440" y="250" class="dg-sub">normal force + tipping moments</text>
  <!-- annotation -->
  <text x="40" y="52" class="dg-sub">a: foot half-length along x_F = 0.065 m</text>
  <text x="40" y="70" class="dg-sub">b: foot half-width along y_F = 0.010 m</text>
  <text x="40" y="220" class="dg-sub">CoP must remain inside</text>
  <text x="40" y="236" class="dg-sub">the shaded rectangle:</text>
  <text x="40" y="258" class="dg-math">|x_cop| ≤ a, |y_cop| ≤ b</text>
</svg>
<figcaption><span class="figno">Figure 2</span>Top view of the rectangular support polygon in the
foot frame. The MIT Humanoid's foot is long and narrow (<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>6.5</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a = 6.5</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">6.5</span></span></span></span>&nbsp;cm, <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b = 1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span>&nbsp;cm), so
the pitch-moment budget dwarfs the roll-moment budget — a fact the constraint matrix must encode
per axis, in the correct frame.</figcaption>
</figure>

<p>
The center of pressure is the point on the sole where the contact pressure distribution
resolves to a pure force. With the wrench taken about the foot origin,
</p>

<div class="eq"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">c</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">o</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi></mrow><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mfrac><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>y</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub></mfrac><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="2em"/><msub><mi>y</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">c</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">o</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi></mrow><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub></mfrac><mo separator="true">,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x_{\mathrm{cop},F} = -\frac{M_{y,F}}{F_{z,F}},
\qquad
y_{\mathrm{cop},F} = \frac{M_{x,F}}{F_{z,F}},</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" class="mpunct">,</span></span></span></span></span></div>

<p>
(a pitch-forward moment moves the pressure toward the heel; a roll moment moves it laterally —
the signs follow from <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="bold">M</mi><mo>=</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="bold">r</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">c</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">o</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi></mrow></msub><mo>×</mo><mi mathvariant="bold">F</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbf{M} = \mathbf{r}_{\mathrm{cop}} \times \mathbf{F}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6861em;"></span><span class="mord mathbf">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8694em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">cop</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6861em;"></span><span class="mord mathbf">F</span></span></span></span>). Physical
validity of the contact is precisely the CoP remaining inside the sole rectangle:
</p>

<div class="eq"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mo>−</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>≤</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">c</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">o</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi></mrow><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo>≤</mo><mi>a</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="2em"/><mo>−</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>≤</mo><msub><mi>y</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">c</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">o</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi></mrow><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo>≤</mo><mi>b</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">-a \le x_{\mathrm{cop},F} \le a,

<p>
These are ratios of decision variables — nonlinear as written. But stance already guarantees
<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo>&gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">F_{z,F} &gt; 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9694em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">F</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.044em;">z</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">F</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&gt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span> through the normal-force bound, so multiplying through by <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">F_{z,F}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9694em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">F</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.044em;">z</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">F</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> is a legal,
<em>exact</em> linearization (not an approximation):
</p>

<div class="eq"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mo>±</mo><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo>−</mo><mi>b</mi><mtext> </mtext><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo>≤</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="2em"/><mo>±</mo><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>y</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo>−</mo><mi>a</mi><mtext> </mtext><msub><mi>F</mi><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>F</mi></mrow></msub><mo>≤</mo><mn>0.</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\pm M_{x,F} - b\,F_{z,F} \le 0,
